#####

Old Phone will be rejected during pickup if

*   * Phone is not in working condition
  * RAM/Storage/IMEI do not match or verification on Rabbit Exchange App fails
  * Screen lock or icloud lock is not disabled.
  * Phone has damages on body (bends, dents, cracks, scratches, loose panel) or screen (discoloration, dead pixels, cracks, spots, lines, traces of replacement)

#####

Exchange tip

  * If old phone is rejected during pickup, you can pay the exchange discount amount at the time of delivery by card or cash and keep the new phone
  * The “Limited-Time Discount” will not be refunded if the old item is successfully picked up

##  1 Year Screen Damage Protection Plan

from Acko

[ __](/product-
reviews/B0DW9GF6L1/ref=psd_bb_r1_B0DC8F2X6T_B0DW9GF6L1?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=1)
[ (4) ](/product-
reviews/B0DW9GF6L1/ref=psd_bb_r1_B0DC8F2X6T_B0DW9GF6L1?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=1)

  * Plan is valid from the date of purchase till 1 year.
  * Plan is email delivered and auto activated if purchased along with mobile on Amazon.
  * Wear and tear, theft, accessories, intentional damages, and brand warranty exclusions are not covered
  * plan is not valid if purchased standalone.
  * How to raise a repair request: Option A: Go to Acko.com >> Enter your mobile number >> file repair. Option B: Download Acko mobile app >> Enter your mobile number >> file repair. Option C: Go to Your Orders on Amazon app >> Get Product Support >> Schedule a repair. Plan is applicable for Samsung, Mi, OnePlus, OPPO, Vivo, Realme, iQoo and Tecno phones only

##  10 days Service Centre Replacement

Replacement Reason  |  Replacement Period  |  Replacement Policy   
---|---|---  
Defective Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  Nothing warranty policy (at Service Centre)   
Physical Damage,  
Wrong and Missing Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  Replacement   
  
__

Defective item:

  * Amazon may provide support via self-help guides or on call or at doorstep, as applicable. 
  * If this issue is not resolved, please contact Nothing or visit the Service Centre.
  * Nothing will repair the product or provide a replacement or Defective certificate, as applicable. The time taken for resolution will be as per Nothing warranty policies.
  * Please check for nearest Brand service center in your location. For details [ click here ](https://www.amazon.in/gp/help/customer/display.html?ie=UTF8&nodeId=202064020)

  
Physical Damage, Wrong, Missing Items:

  * Returns will not be accepted if it is an Open Box Delivery order
  * Remote verification by image/video will be done by Amazon

verification. Please visit the nearest Nothing Service Centre for product-
related issues. Further support will be provided by the brand at their service
centre as per their warranty policies.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we
don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how
recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also
analyses reviews to verify trustworthiness.

### Customers say

Customers praise the phone's high-end quality, eye-catching design, and good
value for money. The camera receives positive feedback, with one customer
noting it performs well in daylight, and customers find the user interface
satisfactory. The phone's performance is smooth, though charging speed and
battery life receive mixed reviews - while some find it fast, others report
slow charging and fast draining.

[![](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-
pixel.gif)Amazon Customer](javascript:void\(0\))

 _5 out of 5 stars_

##### Amazing software and design.

The title sums up the entire review but there is a breakdown: First, the
software. It is so clean and smooth. Nothing OS has become my favourite UI
now. The optimization that Nothing has done with their phones is just amazing.
UI feels so smooth to use, lots of customisation features and overall feels
polished. The phone is surprisingly light and comfortable to hold. I love the
design so much and the uniform bezels at the front is just the cherry on top.
It's a 6.7 inch phone but it doesn't feel large to hold which is a good thing.
The back is a fingerprint magnet though so you'd need a case or just apply a
membrane on the back if you like your phone case free. But use a case with a
membrane if you want to resell it in the future. The battery life is amazing
too. If you don't game too much it'll last you a day and a half which I have
personally experienced, 6- 9 hours of screen on time. No charger inside the
box so I'd recommend getting the original Samsung 25 watt which costs around
1k. It charges the phone under an hour. You can also get the cmf 65 watt
charger but it's on the pricer side. The cameras are surprisingly good too,
not the best but gets the job done. You get stereo speakers and they're pretty
loud too. I've seen better speakers on Motorola phones but it is not bad
either. Haptics are decent too. I've experienced no issues with the network
connectivity, I'm getting 5G++ in my area and the 5G range is amazing too.
Overall, it's a good all round phone. It doesn't beat the competition in the
price range but it provides a good all-round package. Highly recommended if
you want an amazing software experience and design.

##### [ _5.0 out of 5 stars_ Amazing software and design. ](/gp/customer-
reviews/R36RYHK442BTZ6/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 4 July 2025

Verified Purchase

The title sums up the entire review but there is a breakdown:  
First, the software. It is so clean and smooth. Nothing OS has become my
favourite UI now. The optimization that Nothing has done with their phones is
just amazing. UI feels so smooth to use, lots of customisation features and
overall feels polished.  
  
The phone is surprisingly light and comfortable to hold. I love the design so
much and the uniform bezels at the front is just the cherry on top. It's a 6.7
inch phone but it doesn't feel large to hold which is a good thing. The back
is a fingerprint magnet though so you'd need a case or just apply a membrane
on the back if you like your phone case free. But use a case with a membrane
if you want to resell it in the future.  
  
The battery life is amazing too. If you don't game too much it'll last you a
day and a half which I have personally experienced, 6- 9 hours of screen on
time. No charger inside the box so I'd recommend getting the original Samsung
25 watt which costs around 1k. It charges the phone under an hour. You can
also get the cmf 65 watt charger but it's on the pricer side.  
  
The cameras are surprisingly good too, not the best but gets the job done.  
  
You get stereo speakers and they're pretty loud too. I've seen better speakers
on Motorola phones but it is not bad either. Haptics are decent too.  
  
I've experienced no issues with the network connectivity, I'm getting 5G++ in
my area and the 5G range is amazing too.  
  
Overall, it's a good all round phone. It doesn't beat the competition in the
price range but it provides a good all-round package. Highly recommended if
you want an amazing software experience and design.

##### [ _5.0 out of 5 stars_ Overall A Good Phone For The Price 👍
](/gp/customer-reviews/R8JUGP3USECQQ/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 5 July 2025

Verified Purchase

The Nothing Phone 2a Plus is honestly a really nice phone. It looks super
clean and aesthetic, definitely stands out in the crowd. The processor is
smooth and handles daily tasks easily. You can do some average gaming too
without any major issues. It’s well-optimised and doesn’t feel like it’ll go
outdated too quickly.  
  
The camera is quite good, even the nighttime shots come out nicely. Only thing
is the front camera could be a little better in low light. Also, the back
panel tends to catch scratches if you don’t use a case so that’s something to
watch out for.  
  
Overall, for ₹22,000, it’s a solid deal. Great design, good performance, and
worth the price.

clean and aesthetic, definitely stands out in the crowd. The processor is

##### [ _4.0 out of 5 stars_ Good mobile phone ](/gp/customer-

Reviewed in India on 24 November 2024

Verified Purchase

I have using this phone around for 2 months and here is the review form my
side.  
  
Although u will get another brand phone with more specification for this price
but I bought because of their software experience.And everyone is asking is
this iPhone as the side looke and looking without focusing backside this phone
is completely and iPhone inspired design 😁  
  
The body quality is average in my experience as the frame and back panel is
getting scratches even though I put safety case.  
  
You have to buy charger as this come without charging adaptor in the box. U
have to spent almost 1k for that. This is a cons.  
  
If u r using phone continuously u will get around 1-1 1/2 days battery with
battery saver on.  
But if u need 120Hz refresh rate then u have to use without battery saver
which reduces ur battery more often.  
  
Display quality is good. In display finger print also works smooth.  
  
Gaming experience is average as this processor is not meant for heavy gaming
purpose.  
  
Camera quality is also average so don't expect much from camera side although
it has 50mp it is completely worthless  
  
The phone doesn't have that much weight so easy to handle.  
  
If u need nice software experience u can buy this phone or else u can look for
another in this budget. Dont expect much from this phone as it is below
Nothing phone (2) level so if u have some more budget u can go for that.  
Or u can buy nothing phone (2a) as there is not much difference for this phone
and 2a.  
Thank you 😊
